Erika, the nicest woman who works in the front, walked me through all availability, proposed the best offers and was willing to go the extra mile to get me a storage space for not much smaller while being $450 less.
Erika went above and beyond to accommodate me as a long term client preventing me from relocating. She was patient and had a sense of humor while maintaining a high level of professionalism.
If you want great space within the city so that you have quick access, this location is perfect! Pricing is reasonable, location is clean and they respect your space. < Text>
They only have three carts that are only usable when staff is there to trade your ID for it. So if you have a large amount of moving to do after hours, you're going to have to carry each item to your unit individually. While the staff at the front desk is friendly enough , the policies this place implements feels like they treat their customers like thieving enemies. I was told this was because carts had disappeared in the past. I know the carts are there as a convenience, but I've been to other storage facilities that have a bunch at the ready, no ID exchange required for use.

Also, they will raise your rent 10% within the first 6 months of being there. I was told "you obviously didn't read the fine print".

The place is fine. It's clean. Staff is friendly. If you need to store your stuff, it'll do the trick.<//Text>

Edwin and Afi were great, working tirelessly to ensure a smooth process for signing the lease, procuring the insurance, and moving into the unit.  When I arrived less than 24 hours following signing of the lease to move in however, I found that the elevators in the entire place were down.  Although Edwin and Afi moved swiftly to get the elevator guy (and the key pad key) down to fix the problem on Friday afternoon just before end of month, I have yet to receive any contact from management to offer to mitigate my having had to pay movers to wait around  for 30 minutes until the elevators were fixed.  I mean, the one material thing you need from the storage place on move day is working elevators.</review>

< Review>
Bruce And Jose Are Amazing!

Please, please, give this particular Boomerang's food and service a try, you won't regret it at all! The fried zucchini was the biggest portion for an appetizer I've ever had, the fresh garlic in the mashed potatoes, just perfect, and the chicken wings were very generous in portion size.

The service was something I haven't been given since the 1970's or 80's; so personalized, friendly, and, they just made our short stay like being at home.  And, for me, that means a lot.

I'm going to make Boomerang's a regular stop!< /Review>

<Review>Best burgers I have ever had.

The atmosphere is great, its not what you would expect for how good it is though. They have TVs displaying sports or news or whatever else, which doesn't really bother me one way or the other. The owners are the nicest people. They love to come and talk to you like you were a close friend, which is amazing. They are down to earth, and love to hear your honest feedback. They are always thinking up new ideas to make the customers happier.

Their location is a bit strange, and its easy to miss where you pull in. I am a new driver though, and I could do it easily. The location has a very homey feel to it, which I adore.

So! The food. Their menu, which I heard that they are freshening up a bit, looks a little daunting. It isn't. It is in big font, which makes it easy to read, but makes it look kinda like the menu is bigger than it is. What I got this last time was the make your own burger. You get to choose your meat, cheese, toppings, insides of the burger, your side, the works. I got my burger medium rare, and it was delicious. I have leftovers waiting for me in the fridge it filled me up so well! (They've even won awards as far as I know!)

These wonderful people need to see some more love. They are incredible, and so very sweet. We need to get the news out there about them.

I hope my review helped with the decision to eat there!< /Review>< Pictures>

Darrien Boling<//username>
<Time>1556404544116</Time>< rate>
4</rate>
< review>
Boomerang's is a unique burger joint in the Clairemont Mesa area. It's not very noticeable from the main road, and even from the parking lot, the entrance is hidden away in a little courtyard. First, the criticisms: The building seems older and not well taken care of. This is emphasized by the hodgepodge decorations (but not in a good way). There was also no music (though I did notice ceiling speakers), which contributed to making the ambiance awkwardly quiet since there were few guests when we went and the restaurant is surprisingly large. On the positive side, our waiter (Jose) was very friendly and attentive. I had a 1/2lb Bad Breath Burger with Chilli Pepper Onion Rings. I love garlic; so, having garlic mixed into the Patty was amazing. Staying true to it's name, the cheese of choice is gorgonzola, and it is slathers with just enough fresh horseradish. Grilled onions galore top the creation, and on the side comes a creamy garlic-horseradish mayo. The Chilli Pepper Onion Rings have a wonderful crunch and get an added kick by the jalapeno topping. It comes with habanero ketchup which is good, though not as spicy as I hoped for, given the name. Overall, it's a delicious meal in an okay space. But, I think it's worth a shot!<//review>

< Review>
Sakuraya is a clean modern Japanese restaurant found near the infamous Pacific Ranch Market in Orange.

They offer sushi/sashimi, entree plates/bowls and dinner combinations.  I recommend anything that includes the don katsu...it is crisp and delicious.  The don katsu entree and curry bowl are my two favorite choices.  Drop in for lunch, and their 2 choice menu item is a bargain!

If you are in the mood for sushi, a sushi bar is available with friendly chefs serving things up.

Alcohol in the form of beer, wine and sake is available.< /Review>

<Text>This is one of the few bars in LA where I can actually stay until closing! They have a beautiful view of the city which is going to hard to come by with all the construction happening off sunset.There is a entrance on Sunset, that only sometimes has a doorman, don't know why...b but you can easily enter through the Mondrian entrance. Just head straight back and it will be on your right. there are plenty of couches outside and a smaller covered seating area generally reserved for parties/bottle service, by the bar. The waiters and hostesses are friendly. Restrooms are "downstairs" to your left, or straight ahead when you first enter through the roped off entrance. Drinks are a bit pricey, but they are heavy pours..how I have not seen someone drunk fall into the pool or tumble down the stairs I don't know.
